Done. I created `/lib/utils.sh` with the requested functions and sourced it, then ran the demonstrations.

### `/lib/utils.sh` contents
```bash
#!/usr/bin/env bash

to_upper() {
  tr '[:lower:]' '[:upper:]'
}

count_lines() {
  local file="$1"
  wc -l < "$file"
}

file_size() {
  local file="$1"
  wc -c < "$file"
}
```

### Demonstration output
- `printf 'hello world\n' | to_upper` → `HELLO WORLD`
- `count_lines /data/sample.txt` → `5`
- `file_size /data/sample.txt` → `49`

Done — I created `/scripts/start.sh` and ran it in both scenarios.

### `/scripts/start.sh`
```bash
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail

DB_HOST_WAS_SET="${DB_HOST+x}"

DB_HOST_RESOLVED="${DB_HOST-localhost}"
DB_PORT_RESOLVED="${DB_PORT-5432}"
DB_NAME_RESOLVED="${DB_NAME-myapp}"
LOG_LEVEL_RESOLVED="${LOG_LEVEL-info}"

echo "DB_HOST=${DB_HOST_RESOLVED}"
echo "DB_PORT=${DB_PORT_RESOLVED}"
echo "DB_NAME=${DB_NAME_RESOLVED}"
echo "LOG_LEVEL=${LOG_LEVEL_RESOLVED}"

if [[ "$DB_HOST_WAS_SET" == "x" ]]; then
  echo "custom_db=true"
fi
```

### Run results

**1) No env vars set**
```text
DB_HOST=localhost
DB_PORT=5432
DB_NAME=myapp
LOG_LEVEL=info
```

**2) With `DB_HOST=db.prod.internal`**
```text
DB_HOST=db.prod.internal
DB_PORT=5432
DB_NAME=myapp
LOG_LEVEL=info
custom_db=true
```

Here’s a Bash script that does exactly what you asked:

```bash
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

UPLOADS_DIR="/uploads"
declare -A counts

# Include hidden files; if no match, glob expands to nothing
shopt -s dotglob nullglob

for file in "$UPLOADS_DIR"/*; do
  # Only process regular files in /uploads (top-level)
  [[ -f "$file" ]] || continue

  name="$(basename "$file")"

  # Determine extension
  # Rules:
  # - If no extension (or trailing dot), use "other"
  # - Hidden files like ".bashrc" => other
  # - Hidden files like ".env.local" => local
  stripped="${name#.}"  # remove one leading dot for extension detection

  if [[ "$name" == *"." && "$name" != "." && "$name" != ".." && "$name" != *"." ]]; then
    ext="other"
  elif [[ "$name" == *"." ]]; then
    ext="other"
  elif [[ "$stripped" == *.* ]]; then
    ext="${name##*.}"
  else
    ext="other"
  fi

  dest_dir="$UPLOADS_DIR/$ext"
  mkdir -p "$dest_dir"

  mv -- "$file" "$dest_dir/"
  ((counts["$ext"]++))

  echo "moved: $name -> $ext/"
done

# Summary (sorted by extension)
for ext in $(printf '%s\n' "${!counts[@]}" | sort); do
  echo "$ext: ${counts[$ext]} files"
done
```

### Save and run
```bash
chmod +x organize_uploads.sh
./organize_uploads.sh
```
